  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_2b66d018-d18f-4c99-b22a-1ebcbf291738'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"

The one time she’s allowed there during club hours she runs into Asher Mayson. He’s perfect until he opens his mouth and makes assumptions. November wants nothing to do with Asher but too bad for November, fate has other plans. <br /><br />Asher Mayson has never had a problem getting a woman, that is until November.               <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=bad-boys">bad-boys</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=rich-guys">rich-guys</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=2017-reads">2017-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=hot-male-characters">hot-male-characters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=new-adult-contemporary">new-adult-contemporary</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1897435078" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15153991688803516259"><b>1 Star</b><br/><br/>I'm sorry but I was disappointed.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1486284381ra/21900167.gif' width='400' height='250' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Where do I begin?<br/><br/><b>November</b>, a girl who grew up in New York, moved to Tennessee when she was fed-up with her abusive single mom and was randomly attacked by a stranger. In her new home she finally reunited with her long-lost father. Eventually, she started working for his club, not as a stripper but as an office worker. There, she met the hottest guy on the planet-- <b>Asher James Mayson</b>, who has siblings that are equally hot. Asher is not only irresistible but </span>
  <span id="freeText15153991688803516259" style="display:none"><b>1 Star</b><br><br>I'm sorry but I was disappointed.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1486284381ra/21900167.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Where do I begin?<br><br><b>November</b>, a girl who grew up in New York, moved to Tennessee when she was fed-up with her abusive single mom and was randomly attacked by a stranger. In her new home she finally reunited with her long-lost father. Eventually, she started working for his club, not as a stripper but as an office worker. There, she met the hottest guy on the planet-- <b>Asher James Mayson</b>, who has siblings that are equally hot. Asher is not only irresistible but he has also a bad-boy personality which made her totally smitten. He's also rich as he owns a security company. And then... they fell in love. Then things start to get crazy as November's attacker followed her and made her life miserable.<br><br>So, there was <b>insta-love</b> here. And I hated it because it's super duper insta-love! When Asher called her <i>"baby"</i> on their first date I was like, WTH?<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1486285479ra/21900311.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And then he's got all-protective Alpha and jealous even if they're still new and that's it. I was so annoyed. His approach was manipulative. He treated November as if she doesn't have the right to decide and the right to refuse. What. The. Actual. Fuck.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1486286909ra/21900500.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And then he kidnapped her (like literally!) because he's "interested". Seriously? And not only that. He even took her phone and keys so she can't get away from him. What a creep!<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"I'm not ready to have you out of my sight."<br><br>"Why?"<br><br>"Because I'm interested."<br><br>"I'm sure." I roll my eyes. "So if you're interested, then why not ask me out like a normal guy instead of basically kidnapping me?"<br><br>"Why, if I asked you out, you would have blown me off and avoided me. This way, you don't have a choice. I have your keys and your phone."<br><br>"You have my phone?" I screech, opening my bag to see if he's telling the truth. "How did you get my phone? Oh my God, you're insane. I'm driving down a dark road with an insane person who kidnapped me."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>And don't even get me started on the cheese and the predictable plot twist.<br><br>Thanks for the lots of patience I was able to finish it, but not without me rolling my eyes at least 20 times. *sigh<br><br><blockquote>
  <p>
    <a href="https://pagesofpearl.wordpress.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
      <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1472382775i/20186886._SX540_.jpg" alt="Pages of Pearl" width="400" height="150" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
    </a>
  </p>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1464648592i/19260109.png" width="250" height="180" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

<div id="review_874154665" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/874154665" />
    <a title="Candace" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/16384209-candace"><img alt="Candace" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1459720769p2/16384209.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/874154665?book_show_action=true">Feb 18, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Candace" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Candace" href="/user/show/16384209-candace">Candace</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/18524249-until-november">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=hate-that-i-love-them">hate-that-i-love-them</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=pregnant-heroines">pregnant-heroines</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=listened-to-audio-version">listened-to-audio-version</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=sweet-heart-warming-stories">sweet-heart-warming-stories</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=shocking-twists">shocking-twists</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer874154665" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2893531146428211440">'Until November' has been sitting on my TBR for what seems like forever. I'd been meaning to start this series, but just never quite got around to it. When the audiobook went on sale, I decided to take the plunge with this one.<br/><br/>November has left New York City and headed south to live with her father following a brutal attack. She can't escape the feeling that she's being watched and hunted. Even when she arrives in her father's town, the eerie feeling hangs with her.<br/><br/>Glad to have her in his life, </span>
  <span id="freeText2893531146428211440" style="display:none">'Until November' has been sitting on my TBR for what seems like forever. I'd been meaning to start this series, but just never quite got around to it. When the audiobook went on sale, I decided to take the plunge with this one.<br /><br />November has left New York City and headed south to live with her father following a brutal attack. She can't escape the feeling that she's being watched and hunted. Even when she arrives in her father's town, the eerie feeling hangs with her.<br /><br />Glad to have her in his life, November's father arranges to have her work at the club that he owns with his brother. He wants November to manage the bookkeeping and financial side of the operation, steering clear of the club during the nighttime. He may own a strip club, but he won't have his daughter hanging around during the busy hours (hypocritical much?).<br /><br />When November first meets Asher Mayson, he is a total asshat. He's rude, presumptive and completely out of line. In fact, he's pretty much a domineering jerk for most of the book. Luckily, I love an a$$hole and Asher really grew on me.<br /><br />It turns out that despite being a jerk, Asher is quite the Alpha-male protector as well. That comes in handy when the threats against November start to escalate. It quickly becomes clear that her fears weren't unfounded. Somebody is out to get her.<br /><br />Along with Asher, comes a bevy of sexy brothers. Each of them is instantly willing to protect November as one of their own. It seems that Asher wasn't the only one that had a bad case of "insta-love" when he met November. His brothers are equally taken with her, but in an entirely platonic way.<br /><br />Despite the rapid pace with which November and Asher's relationship progressed, I enjoyed this story. Yes, the timeline was a little unbelievable. They had like one date and then they're moving in together. From that point forward, it's family planning and HEAs. <br /><br />To enjoy this story, you have to be able to overlook the insta-love. It wasn't an issue for me this time. On another day, it might have been a problem. I can be a moody reader like that.<br /><br />This book introduces a robust cast of supporting characters. I'm sure that most of them will get their own books later in the series. Aside from Asher's sexy siblings, there's a brief mention of November's cousins. Her crazy mother and ex-fiancé also play an important role in this book. (Let's just say her mother won't be getting any "mother of the year" awards anytime soon.) <br /><br />Eventually, everything comes to light and the mystery surrounding the attacks against November is solved. I can't say I was terribly surprised with the way it worked out. However, it was still shocking in a "how terrible" sort of way. <br /><br />Although this book is the first in the series, it can easily be read as a standalone. It doesn't leave you hanging with any unanswered questions about November and Asher. It will leave you curious about some of the secondary characters and pave the way for their books.<br /><br />Overall, this was a good book for me. It was entertaining if you're in the mood for an over-the-top, controlling Alpha-male type of story. If not, pass on this one until you are. This is the type of story that could swing one way or the other for me, depending upon my mood. <br /><br />I listened to the Audible version and I have to say that I do not recommend the audio. For me, the narration was terrible. I could barely stand Asher's voice. If you're considering the audiobook, listen to the sample. This was one of those times when I wished that I had. I think that I would've liked the book more if I had read it versus listened to the audiobook. Then again, I listen to everything at 2x - 3x speed, so maybe it isn't so bad at the normal rate.<br /><br />Check out more of my reviews at <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.bookaddicthaven.com">www.bookaddicthaven.com</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="2893531146428211440" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_734870353" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/734870353" />
    <a title="Christy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11284813-christy"><img alt="Christy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594293998p2/11284813.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/734870353?book_show_action=true">Oct 05, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer734870353" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1245180445707757504"><b>4-4.5 Asher Lovin’ Stars!</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%203/2f9b819b-f7a4-468c-8a47-3966257d7bbf_zps064bbe5b.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381828578i/5332885.jpg' alt=' photo 2f9b819b-f7a4-468c-8a47-3966257d7bbf_zps064bbe5b.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>This was such an amazingly fun read! I enjoyed it thoroughly! Funny, sexy, and exactly my type of NA read!<br/><br/><br/>The story starts with twenty five year old November moving from her hometown of NYC to live in the south with her father. November isn’t leaving much... her mother is a mess and never really cared for her, and she has an ex-fiancée who, well... it’s a long story. Anyway, November didn’t even know who her father was until she was eighteen. Now she knows him, she w</span>
  <span id="freeText1245180445707757504" style="display:none"><b>4-4.5 Asher Lovin’ Stars!</b><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%203/2f9b819b-f7a4-468c-8a47-3966257d7bbf_zps064bbe5b.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381828578i/5332885.jpg" alt=" photo 2f9b819b-f7a4-468c-8a47-3966257d7bbf_zps064bbe5b.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>This was such an amazingly fun read! I enjoyed it thoroughly! Funny, sexy, and exactly my type of NA read!<br><br><br>The story starts with twenty five year old November moving from her hometown of NYC to live in the south with her father. November isn’t leaving much... her mother is a mess and never really cared for her, and she has an ex-fiancée who, well... it’s a long story. Anyway, November didn’t even know who her father was until she was eighteen. Now she knows him, she wants to spend more time with him. To have a parent who actually loves her and cares about her is something new for her. There was an incident in NY that caused November to move quickly, so theres a little suspense there.<br><br>Then there is Asher Mayson. Asher is the oldest of the four Mayson brothers. They are all good looking guys, and, well, players. When Asher first sets his eyes on November, he knows. Knows she is something special. He is drawn to her beauty, but when he meets her, it’s over. Not only is she beautiful, she is funny, down to earth, and quirky. He is instantly smitten with her, although he doesn’t show it the normal way. Asher is an alpha male, he’s brash, overprotective and a little gruff. I loved how things went down on their first date...<br><i>
  <blockquote>“I realized yesterday that I needed to stake my claim before some stupid fuck got to you. That’s why I did what you called ‘kidnapping’. I like to call that ‘securing my future.’ We’re going to see where this goes, November, and while we’re doing that, it’s not going to be casual.”</blockquote>
</i><br>I am a complete sucker for an alpha male that can make me swoon, and let me tell you- I was in an ASHER FOG the entire time I was reading! Loved this guy! And damn, was he hot! <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%203/dabd21bb-9bec-401b-85a9-37b8ac87ceeb_zps0753db0b.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381828578i/5332886.jpg" alt=" photo dabd21bb-9bec-401b-85a9-37b8ac87ceeb_zps0753db0b.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Asher and November had some amazing chemistry. I loved them together. It is the best feeling for me to love both of the main characters. Of course I loved Asher and his alpha male goodness, who wouldn’t? But I also loved November. She was spunky, funny and sweet. An all around great character, someone you could see yourself being friends with. It was nice to see her befriending Liz, sticking up for herself with the town hussies, and coming into her own. <br><br>Asher and November’s relationship progresses rather quickly. He knows November is it for him... it’s that Mayson curse that hit his father, his grandfather, and it’s finally took hold of him. <br><i>
  <blockquote>“So the Mayson curse is real. Fall in love on sight and all that bullshit. </blockquote>
</i> As happy as November is with Asher and their families, things aren’t perfect for her. Her relationship with her mother is awful, and that incident that happened to her in NY is following her. It gave the element of suspense to the story. Asher knows all about what happened to November, and he won’t let anything touch her again. She is his and he will take care of her, no matter what. He knows November is it for him. <br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“If you left me, I would never be able to find another you. Someone who fills my life with the beauty only you give me.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%203/1703543f-3ccb-4d31-8906-796a10fbbee5_zpsc9d75d6f.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381828578i/5332887.jpg" alt=" photo 1703543f-3ccb-4d31-8906-796a10fbbee5_zpsc9d75d6f.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i>Until November</i> is a fantastic debut novel that incorporates humor, steam, romance and suspense. You will fall in love with Asher and November, along with many of the secondary characters. You will laugh, smile and swoon throughout the story. My only real complaint is that there were times that the timeline jumped ahead too quickly and things felt a bit rushed. I wanted this book to last! The ending was wonderful and I absolutely adored the epilogue! I am so excited that Asher’s younger brother Trevor is getting his own story and I look forward to reading more from this author in the future! <br><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%203/4b432859-1410-4cdc-9764-d3a0600f4bf3_zps300fc80f.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381928394i/5434656.jpg" alt=" photo 4b432859-1410-4cdc-9764-d3a0600f4bf3_zps300fc80f.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><i>
  <blockquote>“It's amazing", he whispered, "to know that my purpose in life is sitting in front of me.” </blockquote>
</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="1245180445707757504" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_840659376" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/840659376" />
    <a title="Natalie" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6092526-natalie"><img alt="Natalie" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1590598261p2/6092526.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/840659376?book_show_action=true">Jan 31, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Natalie" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Natalie" href="/user/show/6092526-natalie">Natalie</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer840659376" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13128637483234422400"><i>I apologise in advance, this is a harsh review of the book. I was angry when I wrote this. It contains spoilers if you've not read the book.</i><br/><br/>This book...<br/><br/><a href='http://tinypic.com?ref=b80f4i' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1394725904ra/8896535.gif' alt='Image and video hosting by TinyPic' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Every page had some type of error. Either it was a spelling mistake, the author wrote one thing in one chapter then changed it in another, or a sentence wouldn't make sense. That really frustrates me, it's making me feel that authors now are getting too lazy to get the book edited properly or they're not even checking it over themselves. We'r</span>
  <span id="freeText13128637483234422400" style="display:none"><i>I apologise in advance, this is a harsh review of the book. I was angry when I wrote this. It contains spoilers if you've not read the book.</i><br><br>This book...<br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=b80f4i" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1394725904ra/8896535.gif" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Every page had some type of error. Either it was a spelling mistake, the author wrote one thing in one chapter then changed it in another, or a sentence wouldn't make sense. That really frustrates me, it's making me feel that authors now are getting too lazy to get the book edited properly or they're not even checking it over themselves. We're spending money on the book and wasting our own time reading something that the author or editor just couldn't be bothered to correct it properly. It's not like it takes long to read it but for me, it took so bloody long. <br><br>It's not just this author, lately all the books I've read have been full of mistakes. Can all authors please spell-check their books please??<br><br>Now, this story sounded good but it was also very misleading to the actual story. <br><br><i>After leaving the Big Apple and her bad memories for Tennessee, November starts working for her dad at his strip club doing the books.</i><br><br>where we see her do work....once? Then she doesn't work again and seems to spend her free time either shopping, having coffee with friends or having sex with Asher.<br><br><i>November wants nothing to do with Asher but too bad for November, fate has other plans. </i><br><br>Misleading. As soon as she see's him she wants him. He asks her out and she says yes, case closed. Not once do I recall her ever thinking she wasn't interested in him, although to be fair he does force her to go on a date with him. <br><br><i>Asher Mayson has never had a problem getting a woman, that is until November.</i><br><br>WRONG. He has no problems with November because she's so willing to do anything for him. He meets her when she's with her dad and he thinks she is one of his strippers and he insults her (love at first sight right there) then her dad introduces November as his daughter THEN he's ~in love~. He bumps into her again when she takes her dog to visit the old people in the elderly home (????) and it happens to be his grandmother who also loves this girl. He forces her to go out with him and the rest is history. No problem with getting her to date him.<br><br><i>Now all he can think about is making November his and keeping her safe.</i> <br><br>From his introduction, it takes about 3 pages for him to 'make November his' so this is dumb.<br><br><br>I can't even... this story was just pointless. A lot of the time I was wondering what the real story was, I know she had some stalker after her but it was more of a side story to her and Asher and their "relationship" - which was a total mess - and when we got to the stalker issue at the end, it was resolved in 2 pages. It was unnecessary drama and it pissed me off. That's one of my book peeves, the author adding drama in when its not even needed, if you have a good story and you can write it properly, you don't need that.<br><br><br>Let me move onto the characters. First off, I knew the girl was called November in the story because it's in the summary and it's also the title of the book. However, I still hated it. Most of the people who talk to her in this book didn't even call her that anyway, they were always calling her 'baby girl' or 'baby' - which also got on my tits. Now November at first came across as a little strange because of this 'talking her to dog' thing and she also came across as naive. She didn't grow at all, none of the characters did but to be fair there wasn't any character development anyway. <br><br>Her first week in Tennessee she decides to take her dog - the one that saved her pissing life in New York - to the old folks home. Who knows if they have allergies or anything but it doesn't matter, she just decides to walk in and show people her dog and act as if she's the most amazing person in the world. (Who does this? Especially if you're new to the area, that wouldn't be your first place to visit) Is she trying to prove something? Whatever it is, it's annoying<br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=34j3s08" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1394725904ra/8896536.gif" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Everyone loves this girl and I can't get my head around it. Guys fancy her and girls want to be her friend. This girl lived in NEW YORK CITY. It's a tough place to live and she's so dumb and weak. If you grow up in a place like New York, you're going to be tough. Not her though, she still needs a guy to keep her safe.<br><br>And let me move onto said guy - Asher Mayson. Psh. I got a Travis Maddox vibe from him. Short tempered, controlling and over protective (the bad kind). He was constantly getting pissy for random and stupid reasons, and he'd use sex as a way to get out of an arguement with November. She'd <i>try</i> and stand up for herself and he'd be like 'NO IT'S THIS, END OF STORY' then he'd kiss her and she'd go into an 'Asher Fog'<br><br><i>Asher Fog</i><br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=jazyoj" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1394727311ra/8896813.gif" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>which basically means whenever he's near, she has no fucking brain. She can't think for herself and without talking the issue they have out, he just fucks her. Arguement over. He uses sex as a way to get his own way because ~she luvs him soooo muchhh and omg he's so good in bedd~<br><br>He's also kind of harsh, he grabs hold of her hair at one point and yanks it mid-arguement, shouts at her to look into her eyes, when she doesn't he shouts "EYES! NOW!"<br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=2zr14yo" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1394727770ra/8896896.gif" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>just little things like that gives me a 'domestic violence' vibe. And what's with this 'coming together' shit, why do they have to 'come together' all the time. Can't she just enjoy it without you having to come with her? It got old and annoying really quickly, the author tried to make it romantic I think. Let the girl enjoy it, if you're really that amazing in bed then maybe you could give her more than one orgasm then you could probably 'come together' at some point. Yeah not that great now are you? Smug bastard.<br><br>She's hardly even allowed to see her friends, if she does then he gives her a hard time. There's no trust at all and he's so suffocating. Why would you want to be with a guy like that? Oh yeah, he has money and he's ~sooo hot~<br><br>Didn't like him at all.<br><br>The other characters were dumb too, forgot all their names and there were too many minor characters with no characteristics that makes you remember them that they're all a blur. They'll be like 'oh let's tell Trevor, then Alice' and I'm like WHO???<br><br>DON'T EVEN GET ME STARTED ON THE EPILOGUE<br><br>SPOILERS but to be fair, I wouldn't even bother with this book. She and Asher have a daughter and she calls it.....................JULY. July Heaven Mayson. JULY. JULY HEAVEN. <br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=16kz91d" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1394727311ra/8896814.gif" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>just...just....<i>ugh</i> and another thing is that she has another FOUR daughters randomly and you know she'll call them fucking March, April, May and June. <br><br>The way the epilogue is written isn't good either, it's so rushed. We hardly know anything and what I've also noticed about this whole book is - and a lot of other people have put this in their review - is that she tells and doesn't show. She fast forwards parts of the book and then she tells us what we've missed. YOU SHOULD BE SHOWING US, WE'RE YOU. Show us when it happens to you. There's all this fuss about her water breaking and everyone's like 'OH NO, HER WATER BROKE' and they're fussing over her for about 3 pages then it says '9 hours later, I had a daughter called July Heaven'<br><br>....................instead of all that shit about people repeating 100 times that you're water broke, atleast make it interesting and give us a birth scene. So boring. She kept skipping parts that she could of made the book more interesting with and leaving us with boring parts.<br><br><i>16 years later</i> I have 5 daughters and Asher's lyk sooooooo overprotective<br><br>Overkill on the protective father shit, it's him shouting at his daughter about a guy she's seeing and November's laughing. Dumb.<br><br>OH. And it took her THREE MONTHS to realise that she's pregnant. THREE MONTHS. It took her that long to see that she hadn't had a period, she's getting fat and she was sick when she smelt paint on Asher (although she's only sick ONCE when she finds out she's pregnant which I find odd but what do I know? I've never been pregnant). If that were me, I'd notice after I've not had a period for one month let alone three.<br><br>I really can't be bothered to waste my time with this book anymore so I can't be fucked to finish reviewing it as I have a few more points. I really hated it and I was so close to giving up around half way but decided to give it another go. Wish I hadn't.<br><br>1 star. I want my money back. I'm in a reading rut because of so many bad books, if anyone has any good recommendations, please let me know. Thank you!</span>
  <a data-text-id="13128637483234422400" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_732153839" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/732153839" />
    <a title="Jamie" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11971939-jamie"><img alt="Jamie" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1450934094p2/11971939.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

  <b> 5 ASHER FOG STARS!!</b>
</i><br><br><i>

</i><br><br><i>When the book starts off we are introduced to November and her savior "Beast". She's been through a world of shit and is leaving the big city moving to Tennessee to live with her dad. A dad that she didn't know growing up with due to the most heinous bitch of a mom. November nearly lost her life, and if it hadn't been for a stray dog saving her.. she would have. Beast is all she has right now. She needs a fresh new start and she can't get that living in constant fear of what may happen next.. so her and Beast are getting the hell out...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381078229i/4108488._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Asher Asher Asher *dreamy lustful sigh*.. ok, I drooled quite a bit over Asher. He's my favorite type of book boyfriend. Total alpha and possessive. Takes not shit and goes after what he wants. When he lays eyes on November he wants her right away but holds back at first due to a "slight" misunderstanding.. but once that's cleared up, and it clears up pretty quick, he's not going to let anything keep him from November. Not even November herself.</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381079108i/4111420.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>November never stood a chance against Asher, and honestly..she never really put up too much of a fight. Hell, I would have rolled over and asked him to rub my hoohah the first time I met him! Asher is just sex on a stick. And a very talented stick at that... ;)<br><br><i>
  <b>“You’re mine. Every inch of you belongs to me. From your sweet mouth to your even sweeter pussy and when I want it, you better give it to me.”<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381080378i/4116517._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>“I love this pussy, baby. So pink, wet, and mine.” He growls the words against my clit, making my pulse race. He licks me from top to bottom. “Jesus, so fucking sweet,” he says, licking me again. This time, his tongue circles my clit, not making contact. I whimper.</b>
</i><br><br>They were so freaking hot together! Aurora knows how to write some seriously steamy sexy times and she doesn't skimp on the details..the scenes between Asher and November where sexy..not dirty. You felt the connection they had. It was more than just sex with these two from the first time. <br><br>As Asher and November are falling deep.. it becomes obvious that the shit November left behind has followed her to Tennessee. Asher's not about to let anything come between what's his, and November is definitely HIS.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381082036i/4122230.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>This book was so easy to read and I didn't want to put it down. It was fast paced with no drag time at all and there was ZERO angst. I loved it. <br><br>I cannot wait for the next book in this series with Trevor. Aurora has introduced us to plenty of sexy alpha's in this first book and there is tons of potential for an excellent series. I am soooo looking forward to the ride. Aurora hit a home run, in my opinion, with this first book. What a way to throw it down girl!! You've got a fan in me and I can't wait to see what you give us next!!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1381082414ra/4123674.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br></span>

And in the perfect caveman style, he hauls her to his house where he has no intention of allowing her to escape.<br><br>Although Asher is a complete alpha-male, November is not a complete push over… unless he uses his mouth to put her in an <b>Asher Fog</b>. November was such a lovable heroine that was completely relatable and utterly adorable without even a trace of being annoying. It is rare these days to come across a heroine that is written to be anything that resembles a functioning, mature adult – but November, even with her hang ups on having a crap mother was every bit a grown ass woman with a backbone.<br><br>Asher had a great balance of the dirty boy and a romantic. </i> <br><br>I can’t believe that this is her first novel… I don’t think there was one thing about this story that I did not absolutely love. A completely well written and executed love story. The dirty talk, sexiness and humor never felt forced, everything just fit perfectly. The only people that might love this book more than those reading it, might be the ones that get to enjoy the after effect of reading this. <br><br><br><br><br></span>

  <b>
    <i>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br/><br/>'From the time I was young, my father and grandfather told me and my brothers that we were cursed. They said that we would only find one love. When we met the woman who was ours, it would be like an explosion. Nothing else would matter but her.'<br/><br/>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379794785i/596848._SX540_.jpg' width='405' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383808093i/6673535._SY540_.jpg' width='350' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br/><br/>“If you left me, I would never be able to find</i></b></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText4297434658432266083" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400128i/775030._SX540_.jpg" width="125" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>♥♥♥ 4 Smokin' Hot Alpha Stars ♥♥♥</b><br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1383807910ra/6673511.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>'From the time I was young, my father and grandfather told me and my brothers that we were cursed. They said that we would only find one love. When we met the woman who was ours, it would be like an explosion. Nothing else would matter but her.'<br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379794785i/596848._SX540_.jpg" width="405" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383808093i/6673535._SY540_.jpg" width="350" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>“If you left me, I would never be able to find another you. Someone who fills my life with the beauty only you give me.”<br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>November is moving to Tennessee to stay with her father. That is because she had just been attacked in New York, where she formerly lived with her terrible and mean mother. She's looking to start new at her twenty-five years of age with the dog that saved her life. For the first time in her life, she feels loved and wanted by the family she had never met. Her dad is an amazing and caring man. Nothing like the mother that spent her whole life puting her down. Her father employs November to work on the books of the business he is co-owner of, a strip club. This is were she meets the sinfully sexy and big jerk, Asher Mayson. <br><br>November had a rough childhood. She grew up believing no one wanted her, including her dad, only to discover the contrary. Her mother was keeping her away from him and was always making sure November felt bad about herself. It was horrible. The woman is a total bitch. I'm so glad November is the opposite. She is kind and considering what she went through, quite secure and high spirited. I really liked her. She didn't let people walk all over her, which was entertaining to see when she wasn't fawning over Asher like every woman in town. But she definitely was attracted to him, and I don't blame her one bit. Asher was freaking hot and persistent. I was in an Asher fog right along with her.<br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383808093i/6673536._SY540_.jpg" width="350" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>“It's amazing", he whispered, "to know that my purpose in life is sitting in front of me.”<br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Asher is the oldest of the Mayson brothers and just as much a player as they all seem to be. This is probably because they are all REALLY hot looking guys. Asher sees November for the first time at her father's club while checking out the security, and he automatically assumes things about her that are wrong. After behaving like a total ass towards her, he realizes his error and just walks away. The thing is, he really is interested in her. He isn't going to give up until November is his. <br><br>Asher is a total Alpha. I am talking about him being a freaking caveman. I would be lying if I said I didn't love it. He made my panties incinerate. Asher is quite successful in what he does. He is possessive, tenacious, domineering, and very protective. I freaking LOVED him. He did at times become a little too much I will admit, but then he would work that charm of his and I was instantly in the Asher fog. I really didn't want to get out of it. He knows that November is the one and is determined to make her see it. He could also be really sweet at times and had me swooning hard. Oh, and I forgot to mention, he had a dirty mouth which was really HOT!<br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1383879587ra/6694634.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>"Your're mine. Every inch of you belongs to me. From your sweet mouth to your even sweeter pussy and when I want it, you better give it to me."<br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>The chemistry between these two characters is undeniable and scorching. They fell in love quite fast, well, at least on Asher's side. November resisted a bit with her heart due to the experience she had with her ex-fiancé. Yes, it was a bit too fast for me, but for some reason, I felt like it worked for them. The pace could have gone a lot quicker, so I'm glad it went on at a steady pace, or I wouldn't have liked it. Not that I have ever had an issue with insta-love. But there have been a few cases where it has bothered me. Here, I actually liked it. Their relationship was an entertaining one to read. As well as the relationships they had with their family members. I really liked all the characters. <br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1383879587ra/6694635.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>"Happy is not the word I would use to describe how I feel, baby."<br><br>"I know," I whisper. "This is bliss."<br><br>"Yeah," he says, walking towards me. "This is bliss." His hands frame my face and he softly kisses my nose then my lips.<br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>The whole book was really great, but it was not perfect. There were a few things that I didn't like about it. One major one being, that I would have liked there to have been some indication that time had passed. You start reading that they are in one place and then suddenly they are at another location and you didn't even know how they got there. I thought I was miss read, but then realized that the book is just like that. That was the only major thing, otherwise I loved both main characters a LOT! The ending was really awesomely sweet. The epilogue had me smiling and laughing at Asher's predicament. But it was really great. I really enjoyed it. And I am so looking forward to all the future books in this series. I can't freaking wait for Trevor's book. I recommend this book to people who love Alpha males.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379794785i/596848._SX540_.jpg" width="405" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

<div id="review_1876829531" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1876829531" />
    <a title="Dilek VT" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/49572641-dilek-vt"><img alt="Dilek VT" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1448923258p2/49572641.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1876829531?book_show_action=true">Feb 08, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Dilek VT" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Dilek VT" href="/user/show/49572641-dilek-vt">Dilek VT</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/49572641-dilek-vt?shelf=dnf">dnf</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/49572641-dilek-vt?shelf=asshole-hero">asshole-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/49572641-dilek-vt?shelf=doormat-heroine">doormat-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/49572641-dilek-vt?shelf=yes-really-that-bad">yes-really-that-bad</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1876829531" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1475854877595883577">Having fed up with today's creepy romance tropes, I have been checking the books published between 2012-2016, hoping I could find better romance books but alas, I have come across another disaster!<br/><br/>This is the 2nd book I have tried from this author and it is once again a DNF! I think I have had enough of her writing and I’m never trying again.<br/><br/>***********************************************<br/><br/><b>DNF after the first 3 chapters! (Yeah, it is that bad!)</b><br/><br/>I know this book has a high rating but you should real</span>
  <span id="freeText1475854877595883577" style="display:none">Having fed up with today's creepy romance tropes, I have been checking the books published between 2012-2016, hoping I could find better romance books but alas, I have come across another disaster!<br /><br />This is the 2nd book I have tried from this author and it is once again a DNF! I think I have had enough of her writing and I’m never trying again.<br /><br />***********************************************<br /><br /><b>DNF after the first 3 chapters! (Yeah, it is that bad!)</b><br /><br />I know this book has a high rating but you should really check 1-star reviews before buying this book. It is just so bad that I cannot even find words to describe it.<br /><br />***<br /><br />If you love alpha-males or if you love obsessive - possessive - dominant men and believe that this book will deliver it, please be forewarned that the writer has a twisted understanding of these concepts as she has created a creepy, over the top and overbearing caveman, instead.<br /><br />***<br /><br />When he first sees the heroine, he thinks she is a stripper and behaves rudely towards her. He acts like a total as*hole. He thinks that she is sleeping with the old man he saw her with in the club. As she called her "daddy", he assumes that he is her "sugar daddy".<br /><br />When he understands she is the daughter of the owner of the strip club and she’s only doing the books there, he doesn’t even apologize to her – at all! <br /><br />***<br /><br />The second time he sees her, he says, “Meet me at the bar tonight,” and he doesn’t say it is a date, he just says, “for beer and playing pools” and the stupid heroine agrees to it. <br /><br />Wouldn't you expect an apology first from the guy who humiliated you because of his assumptions? This one doesn’t because he is soooooo hot! <br /><br />Yayyy, another spineless heroine who has no self-respect!<br /><br />***<br /><br />In the bar where they meet, she shakes a guy’s hand and he gets all jealous and totally acts like he owns her. Then, his past hook-ups come to the bar and hit on him and she gets jealous and wants to leave the bar. The hero then steals her car keys and her phone and carries her to his car, not letting her go. <br /><br />Is this supposed to be hot – to turn us on or something like that? Because it is totally creepy and borderline pscho behavior. <br /><br />Despite her mild resistance, she is all OK with it– wait for it – yes, OK with it all because he is hot! On the day of their first ridiculous date, he starts to say things like, “I am not letting you go out of my sight.”<br /><br />***<br /><br />I am really fed up with these heroines who lose all sense at the sight of a hot guy. Why do authors create heroines that lack any sign of character or self-respect?<br /><br />So, what's the message here? When the guy is too hot, he can do whatever he likes and women should be OK with it??? What kind of a messed-up romance world does this writer live in? <br /><br />***<br /><br />These were one of the most frustrating first chapters of a romance book and I cannot continue to read the book to see how worse it will get because it is already bad enough to cause me to want to crash my kindle on the wall!<br /><br />***<br /><br />Look… I am OK with insta-love if I can feel it but the writer doesn't even bother to write a dialogue to make us feel the insta-attraction. Also, I am not against an alpha-male and I can even love him if his obsessive/possessive behavior is within certain limits but not reaching creepy levels. This hero, though, was the type of guy all women should stay away no matter how hot he is. <br /><br />I don’t care about the rest of the story or if he protects the girl later from the bad guys or what... she needed to protect herself from guys like the hero who wouldn’t let her make her own choices.<br /><br />***<br /><br />OK, here are some more detailed reviews from readers who managed to read more or all of the book. They might give you a better idea about how bad it is:<br /><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1494575559?book_show_action=false&amp;from_review_page=1">https://www.goodreads.com/review/show...</a><br /><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1897435078?book_show_action=false&amp;from_review_page=1">https://www.goodreads.com/review/show...</a><br /><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/840659376?book_show_action=false&amp;from_review_page=1">https://www.goodreads.com/review/show...</a><br /><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/735365498?book_show_action=false&amp;from_review_page=1">https://www.goodreads.com/review/show...</a><br /><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1232528002?book_show_action=false&amp;from_review_page=1">https://www.goodreads.com/review/show...</a><br /><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/735970539?book_show_action=false&amp;from_review_page=1">https://www.goodreads.com/review/show...</a><br /><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1380427967?book_show_action=false&amp;from_review_page=1">https://www.goodreads.com/review/show...</a><br /><br />There are many more 1-star reviews that will give you all the ridiculous details about the book, so please check them before making a decision.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer3453896598960948014"><b>4 Destined Stars</b><br/><br/>After a tragic event, November moves from NY to Tennessee to live with her father, whom she had only met a few years ago thanks to her bitch of a mother. She is broken and trying to get over the past and start again. <br/>She starts working in her father strip clubs, doing the books and only going there during the day, but one day she gets late and only leaves the club late in the night.<br/>And that’s when she meets Asher, he sees her leaving the club and make the wrong assumptions, so th</span>
  <span id="freeText3453896598960948014" style="display:none"><b>4 Destined Stars</b><br><br>After a tragic event, November moves from NY to Tennessee to live with her father, whom she had only met a few years ago thanks to her bitch of a mother. She is broken and trying to get over the past and start again. <br>She starts working in her father strip clubs, doing the books and only going there during the day, but one day she gets late and only leaves the club late in the night.<br>And that’s when she meets Asher, he sees her leaving the club and make the wrong assumptions, so their relationship doesn’t start on the best terms. <br>But life keeps getting on the way and they meet each other again and things starts to change.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1395786429ra/9045287.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Mayson’s men have a curse: when they fall, they fall hard and nothing can keep them from getting what they want. And Asher wants November and even if she is still broken, he is destined to fight for her and heal her. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1388683472i/7901653.jpg" width="350" height="170" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br> <b>Rating: </b> 4 Stars. <br> <b>Storyline: </b> Pretty good. But if you don’t like insta-love and relationships progressing at the speed of light, this is not for you. Because they fall hard, quick and their relationships grows rather fast. Yeah, awesome!! <br> <b>Writing Style: </b> Dual POV (but mostly female). Completely addictive. I’ve started reading this when I got to bed (yeah, always a bad idea) and well, let just say I that I woke up pretty grumpy due to lack of sleep. But I just couldn’t put it down. <br> <b>Character Development: </b> Asher puts the A in Alpha, so basically I loved him. November was pretty good either and didn’t annoyed me, which believe me, it’s hard. <br>The supportive character was great, I can’t wait to read his brother’s books. But my favorite of them all? Beast! Best dog-character ever. <br> <b>Steam: </b> Hot. <br> <b>HEA: </b>	<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Yes. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_798122555" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/798122555" />
    <a title="SamJ ★Needs a HEA★" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3258936-samj-needs-a-hea"><img alt="SamJ ★Needs a HEA★" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1390412715p2/3258936.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/798122555?book_show_action=true">Dec 23, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="SamJ ★Needs a HEA★" class="user" itemprop="url" name="SamJ ★Needs a HEA★" href="/user/show/3258936-samj-needs-a-hea">SamJ ★Needs a HEA★</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3258936-samj-needs-a-hea?shelf=book-challenge-2014">book-challenge-2014</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3258936-samj-needs-a-hea?shelf=genre-contemporary-romance">genre-contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3258936-samj-needs-a-hea?shelf=read-2014">read-2014</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3258936-samj-needs-a-hea?shelf=2-star-reads">2-star-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3258936-samj-needs-a-hea?shelf=theme-awful-parents-of-a-mc">theme-awful-parents-of-a-mc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3258936-samj-needs-a-hea?shelf=theme-insta-lust-or-love">theme-insta-lust-or-love</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3258936-samj-needs-a-hea?shelf=theme-abusive-parents">theme-abusive-parents</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3258936-samj-needs-a-hea?shelf=theme-abuse-issues">theme-abuse-issues</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3258936-samj-needs-a-hea?shelf=reviewed">reviewed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3258936-samj-needs-a-hea?shelf=awful-misogyny-slut-shaming">awful-misogyny-slut-shaming</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer798122555" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17007069611155111090">Ok, so this was a weird one!<br/><br/>I have seen so many good reviews from friends and groups I am in about this series.<br/><br/>But,there was just something that about this book that I did not connect to!<br/><br/>November - did not get her, she was a bit too "kooky" or she was meant to be. I am not sure. All the jumping up and down and clapping her hands! She was a bit daft too - <a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[ 3 months, 3 months she did not have a period and never wondered about it, even though she was putting on weight and could not f</span></span>
  <span id="freeText17007069611155111090" style="display:none">Ok, so this was a weird one!<br><br>I have seen so many good reviews from friends and groups I am in about this series.<br><br>But,there was just something that about this book that I did not connect to!<br><br>November - did not get her, she was a bit too "kooky" or she was meant to be. I am not sure. All the jumping up and down and clapping her hands! She was a bit daft too - <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ 3 months, 3 months she did not have a period and never wondered about it, even though she was putting on weight and could not fasten her jeans properly. Also, why would she bump into her mother, in a town her mother has either never been to, or not been to in years, and just be like "oh right" when the Mom says she has business with a lawyer in town. When the lawyer in town is dealing with the million dollar inheritance that November is getting from her grandparents! Would you not be slightly suspicious? <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>The insta love!? No. She is moved in within like 2 days of meeting this guy! And we get introduced to loads of ppl near the start, that are pretty much never mentioned again! <br><br><br>It was a weird mix of past and present tense! It even changed within a sentence. It was missing punctuation in points.<br><br>The writing is very disjointed and jumps all over the place. Not only do we have time jumps, when all of a sudden, it is a certain length of time ahead, then we get the case of the character giving us a run down of what has happened,etc, just telling us...ok, I do not mind that, and when done well, is ok. It was not done well here! <br><br>And that is almost constant! When it does not need to be. You do not need to jump ahead half an hour, then go back telling us what happened. For example<br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[
  <i>After Trevor is out of sight, I run to the checkout with Liz falling behind me.<br><br>"You guard the door while I take the test." I tell Liz while walking into the small stall.<br><br>"Let me know if you need me" she says from the other side.<br><br>"Holy shit" I whisper. There is it, proof I wanted is right there in black and white. Okay, pink and white, but it is there in my face, proving that I'm an idiot. I've taken four tests, all different brands, so I know they couldn't all be wrong. When I bought the first one and it came out with a giant plus sign, I left the stall that I had been holding up in.<br><br>With Liz following behind me, we went and bought water from the coffee shop and a few more tests. Now all the tests have been taken......</i>
 <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>It just makes for a jarring and disjointed read, that constantly pulls you out of the story and you are constantly having to readjust your thinking as to what and when something is happening! There was one point I thought I had been missing a chapter...all of a sudden, Trevor and Liz are like best friends, whereas they had not even met just the page before. It just jumped ahead, and it was like "Oh Liz and Trev are tight" and I am just like "since when!?<br><br>Character development is poor! As awful as November's background is, you would expect more from that..how it truly affected her. Did not seem to bother her all that much in all honesty! She seemed more bothered by her Mom sleeping with her finance than any other abuse she suffered as a child!<br><br>And, why, why in some books, does our h have to have nearly every man make a play for her, because she is so different! This town she moved to, weird. Other than her and Liz, it seems every other girl is a slut! A whiny slut. The men are sluts too, but apparently that is ok, because they are MEN! And they can call the other women, bitches and sluts, and treat them like crap, because they are bitches and sluts. The men do not think of themselves as sluts, oh no, because they are MEN! They are never ever going to have a relationship with any of these women they have been sleeping with, because they think they are too good for them, they will wait for the sweet, innocent non slut girl to come along. It is all a bit weird and misogynistic and quite frankly happens far too often in books. It is all rather sad tbh! It just puts me off an author.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1423370012ra/13613790.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1502463046ra/23564429.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>However, I have already bought the next 2 in the series, and shall give them a go and see if it improves!</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="17007069611155111090" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

Why did this guy have to have a hot guy name? Why couldn't his name be Urkel or Poindexter. I mean really, something's just were not fair."</b><br><br>Not just the name was hot, the attitude, body and let's not forget about the brothers.. I know I am not because I see follow up hot guy stories! <br><br><b>"November, these are my brothers. Saving her was none other than Beast a Great Dane that was at the right place at the right time. She wasn't made to feel worthy or to give trust unconditionally. Always in a position to defend herself and worth at the drop of a hat. She is still caring and willing to put her heart on the line. I loved watching November become part of a loving family and bond with her dad. She reaches out to others that she sees herself in and with that finds true friendships.<br><br><span>[image error]</span><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381361152i/4761788.jpg" alt=" photo cgyuityi9-erotic-Paare-Zart-black-and-white-jeans-Couples-sexy-NicePics-Touching-Rubbing-C-romance-sexy-pics-for-guys-nude-a_zps2cc6a06a.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>"What did I tell you, son?" he says, looking at Asher. "When it happens-BOOM!" </b><br><br>Asher has always been a "no need to know your name, you aren't sticking around" type of guy. His parents had always warned him he held the curse and when "The One" entered his life, he would know without a shadow of a doubt. He is alpha in every sense of Tara's definition and isn't afraid to show it..ever!<br><br><span>[image error]</span><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380435232i/879277.jpg" alt=" photo alpha_zps5e08b74f.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>"But if any motherfucker touches you, I will not be happy"</b><br><br>I think their first meeting is one of my favs in a book. A miscommunication leads to a very unhappy Asher, who isn't concerned with the who, what or why. Just the YOU ARE MINE and you don't know it yet.. It wasn't insta-love but it was a connection that could not be ignored and for that I say thank the alpha Gods! <br><br><span>[image error]</span><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381361152i/4761789.jpg" alt=" photo scalephp_zps83c41cb5.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I am an epilogue loving girl and this one delivered full force for me.. I love to see in the future of a couple that I have fallen head over heels for. <span id="freeTextContainer12882772805891425313">** 4.5 stars **<br/><br/>I enjoyed this romance so much! There was a possessive, crazy in love hero and a likable strong heroine. The story reminded me of Kristen Ashley in a good way, there was a nice long story told but no major misunderstandings. The story was sexy and sweet and fun to read. I am excited for the hero's brother's story that comes out next.<br/><br/>Just a warning, there were some editing issues with word usage and misspellings in case that bothers you. </span>

For God's shake!!! It's too early, buddy! Calm down!!!!<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1426251826ra/13992942.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Yes, in some point i learned about the "curse" that follow the Masons men... What was that??? They were players and men-whores until the time that met the one and only woman for them... And with the first look, they just know!!! <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1426251826ra/13992943.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Hmmmmm.... Okay!!! I'll try to accept it!!! But that's weird man!!!!<br><br>But let me talk to you about the plot....<br>November is a girl with a little bit fucked up life... She is moving from New York and go to live with her father for first time in her life, after an attack against her life. You see, her mother was a ruthless bitch who take her away from her father and never aloud her to see him... She doesn't have anything to hold her back there, since her shitty mother didn't ever treat her well and since she caught her fiancee to bed with another woman. Guess who??? That bitch who was calling herself a mother!!! <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1426251826ra/13992944.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br>Oh, yes, i'm not kidding you!!!<br>So her baggages have many shitty things inside which were unbearable and made her with low self-confidence...<br><br>So, she is starting this new life and in some point meet Asher Mason. And their first meeting wasn't good. There was a misunderstanding and the words that they're exchange wasn't really good and all of that were Asher's fault!!!! His assumptions were offensive... <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1426252045ra/13992973.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Don't pressure me guys, i can't tell you more...<br><br>Well, Asher were cocky and with high confidence. He liked women very much and his life was really good. NO problems and this is strange because lately in all this kind of books, everybody has too much problems. I'd like that he didn't have problems... For once that was refreshing!!! <br>But he was having other problems... Especially with November... <br>He was bossy and possesssive. He was soooo jealous with everybody who gets near to her, even his brothers!!! <br>But i will give him extra points because he really loved her and he was extra caring and protective of her... <br>Believe me when i'm saying that was for the best, because the attacks didn't stop to New York city, they followed her there... <br>Somebody is stalking November, who could be??? <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380970666ra/3603084.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br>No, i won't tell you. I already say too much. You have to read it!!!<br><br>First of all, i want to say that i really liked the bond between November and Asher and even his bossy attitude, i loved this guys!!! <br>I liked the November's reactions in that attitude. They were making me laugh every single time...<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1403129915ra/10044218.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Secondly, i would liked to talk to you about Beast. He was two times in the road November's savior and the best companion ever... I love him!!!<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1426251826ra/13992949.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Third, i really liked the other character... They were all amazing! I won't talk about his brothers because i will talk about them in the next books, but his parents and her father were great!!! So was Liz, but... <span id="freeTextContainer10830945582336557857">I read this book after a really angsty 5 book series and let me tell you, this was exactly what I needed to balance it out. I'm really into the bossy alpha men who go after what they want and Asher was perfection. November was a bit of a ditz but she was genuinely a nice person who didn't take too many things seriously. They complimented each other perfectly. I loved that the drama in this book was outside of the relationship and we got to see so much of the book with them together. I never get </span>
  <span id="freeText10830945582336557857" style="display:none">I read this book after a really angsty 5 book series and let me tell you, this was exactly what I needed to balance it out. I'm really into the bossy alpha men who go after what they want and Asher was perfection. November was a bit of a ditz but she was genuinely a nice person who didn't take too many things seriously. They complimented each other perfectly. I loved that the drama in this book was outside of the relationship and we got to see so much of the book with them together. I never get tired of reading about a couple getting to know each other and having fun together. I can see myself re-reading this one a lot. </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer2380882837791827477">After a life riddled with lies and neglect, November is moving home to the father she only recently met. He is everything she had wished for in a parent and after being attacked in New York, she has packed up with the dog that saved her and is finally heading home.<br/><br/>It is a blur initially, meeting family members you never new existed. November is slightly anxious but the overwhelming welcome from her family makes her realize she made the right choice. Taking the job at her dad's work though as an </span>
  <span id="freeText2380882837791827477" style="display:none">After a life riddled with lies and neglect, November is moving home to the father she only recently met. He is everything she had wished for in a parent and after being attacked in New York, she has packed up with the dog that saved her and is finally heading home.<br /><br />It is a blur initially, meeting family members you never new existed. November is slightly anxious but the overwhelming welcome from her family makes her realize she made the right choice. Taking the job at her dad's work though as an accountant was perfect, however he did not tell her it was a strip club. Wanting her protected, he keeps her in the back and working days, but the first night she is introduced she meets Asher Mayson. <br /><br />After initial awkward meeting, Asher feels like he has been kicked in the gut. The second time he meets November it doesn't go off all that well either, but he gets her to agree to go out for a beer later. He realizes that November is hesitant of him and his prowess is well known in town, but he knows in his gut she is the one. When it looks like November needs protection, he is right by her side, even though she tries to push him away. Nobody will hurt November if Asher has anything to do with it, he plans to cherish her like she deserves now he only has to get her to realize how much she means to him.<br /><br />I loved, loved, loved this story. It is intense, dramatic, and oozes chemistry with each turn of the page. November is quirky, funny, and I loved the little geeky references made throughout the story. Asher is passion on a stick, broody, and pure alpha man. I stayed up way way way too late with this one,b ut it was so worth it.</span>

I'm sorry he does and I will be the fan girl waiting patiently for all of them (seriously,you better write about all of them.)</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer18392400540194490888">I really liked this one. It was on my tbr list for a while.   <span id="freeText18392400540194490888" style="display:none">I really liked this one. It was on my tbr list for a while. There was definitely some Kristen Ashley influence throughout, i.e., some of Asher's behavior/lingo (there are numerous "chin lifts" and a scene where he demands "Eyes" like several KA alphas do). Make of that what you will.<br /><br />I really liked November. She had a fun personality and acted with sense and reason. I also really liked Asher, aka the former player who is suddenly punched by Cupid and subsequently becomes all possessive alpha male - not gonna lie, I'm a sucker for that. <br /><br />Overall, the story really flowed well, I devoured it in one sitting, and have already started <i>Until Trevor</i>...so that's always a yay in my book.</span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('/Xp+vNoXA5znqIfFk1V7Qvs7tqY5dkexiWR1fJUJYvpihTfTwXlXwBdc4RNhlqG16Xu5IIj2Qmi0fuwsbw0ifQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('nvuX7wgUMXT21QDo+2lItA/vD+J6Ds3V4fVwcmFmnjwBBN6AE3plKAYhZj4JqpJDHa8AZMuOyAzc7+kim2Leuw==')})
  }
